Farro Light Regular (Farro-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Farro-Light', Everything looks good.

Farro Light Regular (Farro-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Farro' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Farro Light'.

Farro Regular (Farro-Regular.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Farro-Regular', Everything looks good.

MS NID 0, Copyright.

Please verify agains spec.
MS NID 0 is 'Copyright 2018 The Farro Project Authors (https://github.com/grayscaleltd/farro)'
It should follow this structure: 'Copyright (c) XXXX - XXXX /entity/. All rights reserved.'

Farro Medium Regular (Farro-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Farro' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Farro Medium'.

Farro Bold (Farro-Bold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Farro-Bold', Everything looks good.
